IPayError::InvalidMultiplier);\n    58→\n    59→        let merchant_key = ctx.accounts.merchant.key();\n    60→        let owner_key = ctx.accounts.owner.key();\n    61→        let now = Clock::get()?.unix_timestamp;\n    62→\n    63→        let merchant = &mut ctx.accounts.merchant;\n    64→        merchant.owner = owner_key;\n    65→        merchant.name = name.clone();\n    66→        merchant.description = description;\n    67→        merchant.merchant_category = merchant_category;\n    68→        merchant.loyalty_multiplier = loyalty_multiplier;\n    69→        merchant.total_payments = 0;\n    70→        merchant.total_volume = 0;\n    71→        merchant.total_loyalty_distributed = 0;\n    72→        merchant.is_active = true;\n    73→        merchant.created_at = now;\n    74→        merchant.bump = ctx.bumps.merchant;\n    75→\n    76→        let platform = &mut ctx.accounts.platform;\n    77→        platform.total_merchants += 1;\n    78→\n    79→        let mname = name.clone();\n    80→\n    81→        emit!(MerchantRegistered {\n    82→            merchant: merchant_key,\n    83→            owner: owner_key,\n    84→            name,\n    85→            timestamp: now,\n    86→        });\n    87→\n    88→        msg!(\"Merchant '{}' registered! Loyalty: {}x\", mname, loyalty_multiplier as f64 / 100.0);\n    89→        Ok(())\n    90→    }\n    91→\n    92→    pub fn update_merchant(\n    93→        ctx: Context<UpdateMerchant>,\n    94→        name: Option<String>,\n    95→        description: Option<String>,\n    96→        merchant_category: Option<String>,\n    97→        loyalty_multiplier: Option<u16>,\n    98→        is_active: Option<bool>,\n    99→    ) -> Result<()> {\n   100→        let merchant = &mut ctx.accounts.merchant;\n   101→\n   102→        if let Some(n) = name {\n   103→            require!(n.len() <= 32, IPayError::NameTooLong);\n   104→            merchant.name = n;\n   105→        }\n   106→        if let Some(d) = description {\n   107→            require!(d.len() <= 128, IPayError::DescriptionTooLong);\n   108→            merchant.description = d;\n   109→        }\n   110→        if let Some(c) = merchant_category {\n   111→            require!(c.len() <= 32, IPayError::CategoryTooLong);\n   112→            merchant.merchant_category = c;\n   113→        }\n   114→        if let Some(m) = loyalty_multiplier {\n   115→            require!(m >= 100 && m <= 1000, IPayError::InvalidMultiplier);\n   116→            merchant.loyalty_multiplier = m;\n   117→        }\n   118→        if let Some(active) = is_active {\n   119→            merchant.is_active = active;\n   120→        }\n   121→\n   122→        msg!(\"Merchant '{}' updated\", merchant.name);\n   123→        Ok(())\n   124→    }\n   125→\n   126→    // ========================================================================\n   127→    // PAYMENTS + AUTOMATIC LOYALTY (CORE INNOVATION)\n   128→    // ========================================================================\n   129→\n   130→    pub fn process_payment(\n   131→        ctx: Context<ProcessPayment>,\n   132→        amount: u64,\n   133→        memo: String,\n   134→    ) -> Result<()> {\n   135→        require!(amount > 0, IPayError::InvalidAmount);\n   136→        require!(memo.len() <= 64, IPayError::MemoTooLong);\n   137→\n   138→        let merchant = &ctx.accounts.merchant;\n   139→        require!(merchant.is_active, IPayError::MerchantInactive);\n   140→\n   141→        let platform = &ctx.accounts.platform;\n   142→\n   143→        // Step 1: Transfer SOL to merchant\n   144→        let platform_fee = amount\n   145→            .checked_mul(platform.platform_fee_bps as u64)\n   146→            .unwrap()\n   147→            .checked_div(10_000)\n   148→            .unwrap();\n   149→        let merchant_amount = amount.checked_sub(platform_fee).unwrap();\n   150→\n   151→        anchor_lang::system_program::transfer(\n   152→            CpiContext::new(\n   153→                ctx.accounts.system_program.to_account_info(),\n   154→                anchor_lang::system_program::Transfer {\n   155→                    from: ctx.accounts.payer.to_account_info(),\n   156→                    to: ctx.accounts.merchant_wallet.to_account_info(),\n   157→                },\n   158→            ),\n   159→            merchant_amount,\n   160→        )?;\n   161→\n   162→        if platform_fee > 0 {\n   163→            anchor_lang::system_program::transfer(\n   164→                CpiContext::new(\n   165→                    ctx.accounts.system_program.to_account_info(),\n   166→                    anchor_lang::system_program::Transfer {\n   167→                        from: ctx.accounts.payer.to_account_info(),\n   168→                        to: ctx.accounts.platform_wallet.to_account_info(),\n   169→                    },\n   170→                ),\n   171→                platform_fee,\n   172→            )?;\n   173→        }\n   174→\n   175→        // Step 2: Auto-mint loyalty tokens (THE INNOVATION)\n   176→        let base_loyalty = amount\n   177→            .checked_mul(platform.loyalty_points_per_sol)\n   178→            .unwrap()\n   179→            .checked_div(1_000_000_000)\n   180→            .unwrap();\n   181→\n   182→        let loyalty_amount = base_loyalty\n   183→            .checked_mul(merchant.loyalty_multiplier as u64)\n   184→            .unwrap()\n   185→            .checked_div(100)\n   186→            .unwrap();\n   187→\n   188→        if loyalty_amount > 0 {\n   189→            let platform_seeds = &[\n   190→                b\"platform\".as_ref(),\n   191→                &[platform.bump],\n   192→            ];\n   193→            let signer_seeds = &[&platform_seeds[..]];\n   194→\n   195→            token_interface::mint_to(\n   196→                CpiContext::new_with_signer(\n   197→                    ctx.accounts.token_program.to_account_info(),\n   198→                    MintTo {\n   199→                        mint: ctx.accounts.loyalty_mint.to_account_info(),\n   200→                        to: ctx.accounts.payer_loyalty_account.to_account_info(),\n   201→                        authority: ctx.accounts.platform.to_account_info(),\n   202→                    },\n   203→                    signer_seeds,\n   204→                ),\n   205→                loyalty_amount,\n   206→            )?;\n   207→        }\n   208→\n   209→        // Capture keys before mutable borrows\n   210→        let payer_key = ctx.accounts.payer.key();\n   211→        let merchant_key = ctx.accounts.merchant.key();\n   212→        let record_key = ctx.accounts.payment_record.key();\n   213→        let now = Clock::get()?.unix_timestamp;\n   214→        let counter = platform.payment_counter;\n   215→\n   216→        // Step 3: Record payment\n   217→        let payment = &mut ctx.accounts.payment_record;\n   218→        payment.payer = payer_key;\n   219→        payment.merchant = merchant_key;\n   220→        payment.amount = amount;\n   221→        payment.platform_fee = platform_fee;\n   222→        payment.loyalty_earned = loyalty_amount;\n   223→        payment.memo = memo.clone();\n   224→        payment.timestamp = now;\n   225→        payment.payment_index = counter;\n   226→        payment.bump = ctx.bumps.payment_record;\n   227→\n   228→        // Step 4: Update stats\n   229→        let merchant = &mut ctx.accounts.merchant;\n   230→        merchant.total_payments += 1;\n   231→        merchant.total_volume += amount;\n   232→        merchant.total_loyalty_distributed += loyalty_amount;\n   233→\n   234→        let platform = &mut ctx.accounts.platform;\n   235→        platform.total_payments += 1;\n   236→        platform.total_volume += amount;\n   237→        platform.payment_counter += 1;\n   238→\n   239→        emit!(PaymentProcessed {\n   240→            payment_record: record_key,\n   241→            payer: payer_key,\n   242→            merchant: merchant_key,\n   243→            amount,\n   244→            platform_fee,\n   245→            loyalty_earned: loyalty_amount,\n   246→            memo,\n   247→            timestamp: now,\n   248→        });\n   249→\n   250→        msg!(\"Payment: {} lamports | Loyalty: {} iPAY\", amount, loyalty_amount);\n   251→        Ok(())\n   252→    }\n   253→\n   254→    // ========================================================================\n   255→    // SPL TOKEN PAYMENTS (USDC etc.)\n   256→    // ========================================================================\n   257→\n   258→    pub fn process_payment_spl(\n   259→        ctx: Context<ProcessPaymentSpl>,\n   260→        amount: u64,\n   261→        memo: String,\n   262→    ) -> Result<()> {\n   263→        require!(amount > 0, IPayError::InvalidAmount);\n   264→        require!(memo.len() <= 64, IPayError::MemoTooLong);\n   265→\n   266→        let merchant = &ctx.accounts.merchant;\n   267→        require!(merchant.is_active, IPayError::MerchantInactive);\n   268→\n   269→        let platform = &ctx.accounts.platform;\n   270→        let payment_mint_decimals = ctx.accounts.payment_mint.decimals;\n   271→\n   272→        // Step 1: Calculate fee split\n   273→        let platform_fee = amount\n   274→            .checked_mul(platform.platform_fee_bps as u64)\n   275→            .unwrap()\n   276→            .checked_div(10_000)\n   277→            .unwrap();\n   278→        let merchant_amount = amount.checked_sub(platform_fee).unwrap();\n   279→\n   280→        // Step 2: Transfer SPL tokens to merchant\n   281→        token_interface::transfer_checked(\n   282→            CpiContext::new(\n   283→                ctx.accounts.token_program.to_account_info(),\n   284→                TransferChecked {\n   285→                    from: ctx.accounts.payer_token_account.to_account_info(),\n   286→                    mint: ctx.accounts.payment_mint.to_account_info(),\n   287→                    to: ctx.accounts.merchant_token_account.to_account_info(),\n   288→                    authority: ctx.accounts.payer.to_account_info(),\n   289→                },\n   290→            ),\n   291→            merchant_amount,\n   292→            payment_mint_decimals,\n   293→        )?;\n   294→\n   295→        // Transfer platform fee\n   296→        if platform_fee > 0 {\n   297→            token_interface::transfer_checked(\n   298→                CpiContext::new(\n   299→                    ctx.accounts.token_program.to_account_info(),\n   300→                    TransferChecked {\n   301→                        from: ctx.accounts.payer_token_account.to_account_info(),\n   302→                        mint: ctx.accounts.payment_mint.to_account_info(),\n   303→                        to: ctx.accounts.platform_token_account.to_account_info(),\n   304→                        authority: ctx.accounts.payer.to_account_info(),\n   305→                    },\n   306→                ),\n   307→                platform_fee,\n   308→                payment_mint_decimals,\n   309→            )?;\n   310→        }\n   311→\n   312→        // Step 3: Auto-mint loyalty tokens\n   313→        // For SPL payments, use 1:1 ratio with loyalty_points_per_sol scaled by decimals\n   314→        let base_loyalty = amount\n   315→            .checked_mul(platform.loyalty_points_per_sol)\n   316→            .unwrap()\n   317→            .checked_div(10u64.pow(payment_mint_decimals as u32))\n   318→            .unwrap();\n   319→\n   320→        let loyalty_amount = base_loyalty\n   321→            .checked_mul(merchant.loyalty_multiplier as u64)\n   322→            .unwrap()\n   323→            .checked_div(100)\n   324→            .unwrap();\n   325→\n   326→        if loyalty_amount > 0 {\n   327→            let platform_seeds = &[\n   328→                b\"platform\".as_ref(),\n   329→                &[platform.bump],\n   330→            ];\n   331→            let signer_seeds = &[&platform_seeds[..]];\n   332→\n   333→            token_interface::mint_to(\n   334→                CpiContext::new_with_signer(\n   335→                    ctx.accounts.loyalty_token_program.to_account_info(),\n   336→                    MintTo {\n   337→                        mint: ctx.accounts.loyalty_mint.to_account_info(),\n   338→                        to: ctx.accounts.payer_loyalty_account.to_account_info(),\n   339→                        authority: ctx.accounts.platform.to_account_info(),\n   340→                    },\n   341→                    signer_seeds,\n   342→                ),\n   343→                loyalty_amount,\n   344→            )?;\n   345→        }\n   346→\n   347→        // Capture keys before mutable borrows\n   348→        let payer_key = ctx.accounts.payer.key();\n   349→        let merchant_key = ctx.accounts.merchant.key();\n   350→        let payment_record_key = ctx.accounts.payment_record.key();\n   351→        let now = Clock::get()?.unix_timestamp;\n   352→        let counter = platform.payment_counter;\n   353→\n   354→        // Step 4: Record payment\n   355→        let payment = &mut ctx.accounts.payment_record;\n   356→        payment.payer = payer_key;\n   357→        payment.merchant = merchant_key;\n   358→        payment.amount = amount;\n   359→        payment.platform_fee = platform_fee;\n   360→        payment.loyalty_earned = loyalty_amount;\n   361→        payment.memo = memo.clone();\n   362→        payment.timestamp = now;\n   363→        payment.payment_index = counter;\n   364→        payment.bump = ctx.bumps.payment_record;\n   365→\n   366→        // Step 5: Update stats\n   367→        let merchant = &mut ctx.accounts.merchant;\n   368→        merchant.total_payments += 1;\n   369→        merchant.total_volume += amount;\n   370→        merchant.total_loyalty_distributed += loyalty_amount;\n   371→\n   372→        let platform = &mut ctx.accounts.platform;\n   373→        platform.total_payments += 1;\n   374→        platform.total_volume += amount;\n   375→        platform.payment_counter += 1;\n   376→\n   377→        emit!(PaymentProcessed {\n   378→            payment_record: payment_record_key,\n   379→            payer: payer_key,\n   380→            merchant: merchant_key,\n   381→            amount,\n   382→            platform_fee,\n   383→            loyalty_earned: loyalty_amount,\n   384→            memo,\n   385→            timestamp: now,\n   386→        });\n   387→\n   388→        msg!(\"SPL Payment: {} tokens | Loyalty: {} iPAY\", amount, loyalty_amount);\n   389→        Ok(())\n   390→    }\n   391→\n   392→    // ========================================================================\n   393→    // REFUNDS\n   394→    // ========================================================================\n   395→\n   396→    pub fn process_refund(\n   397→        ctx: Context<ProcessRefund>,\n   398→        amount: u64,\n   399→    ) -> Result<()> {\n   400→        require!(amount > 0, IPayError::InvalidAmount);\n   401→\n   402→        let payment = &ctx.accounts.payment_record;\n   403→        require!(amount <= payment.amount, IPayError::RefundExceedsPayment);\n   404→\n   405→        // Transfer SOL back from merchant to payer\n   406→        anchor_lang::system_program::transfer(\n   407→            CpiContext::new(\n   408→                ctx.accounts.system_program.to_account_info(),\n   409→                anchor_lang::system_program::Transfer {\n   410→                    from: ctx.accounts.merchant_owner.to_account_info(),\n   411→                    to: ctx.accounts.payer.to_account_info(),\n   412→                },\n   413→            ),\n   414→            amount,\n   415→        )?;\n   416→\n   417→        // Capture keys before mutable borrow\n   418→        let merchant_key = ctx.accounts.merchant.key();\n   419→        let payer_key = ctx.accounts.payer.key();\n   420→        let payment_key = ctx.accounts.payment_record.key();\n   421→        let refund_key = ctx.accounts.refund_record.key();\n   422→        let now = Clock::get()?.unix_timestamp;\n   423→\n   424→        // Record refund\n   425→        let refund = &mut ctx.accounts.refund_record;\n   426→        refund.merchant = merchant_key;\n   427→        refund.payer = payer_key;\n   428→        refund.original_payment = payment_key;\n   429→        refund.amount = amount;\n   430→        refund.timestamp = now;\n   431→        refund.bump = ctx.bumps.refund_record;\n   432→\n   433→        emit!(RefundProcessed {\n   434→            refund_record: refund_key,\n   435→            merchant: merchant_key,\n   436→            payer: payer_key,\n   437→            original_payment: payment_key,\n   438→            amount,\n   439→            timestamp: now,\n   440→        });\n   441→\n   442→        msg!(\"Refund: {} lamports returned to payer\", amount);\n   443→        Ok(())\n   444→    }\n   445→\n   446→    // ========================================================================\n   447→    // LOYALTY REDEMPTION\n   448→    // ========================================================================\n   449→\n   450→    pub fn redeem_loyalty(\n   451→        ctx: Context<RedeemLoyalty>,\n   452→        loyalty_amount: u64,\n   453→    ) -> Result<()> {\n   454→        require!(loyalty_amount > 0, IPayError::InvalidAmount);\n   455→\n   456→        token_interface::burn(\n   457→            CpiContext::new(\n   458→                ctx.accounts.token_program.to_account_info(),\n   459→                token_interface::Burn {\n   460→                    mint: ctx.accounts.loyalty_mint.to_account_info(),\n   461→                    from: ctx.accounts.user_loyalty_account.to_account_info(),\n   462→                    authority: ctx.accounts.user.to_account_info(),\n   463→                },\n   464→            ),\n   465→            loyalty_amount,\n   466→        )?;\n   467→\n   468→        emit!(LoyaltyRedeemed {\n   469→            user: ctx.accounts.user.key(),\n   470→            merchant: ctx.accounts.merchant.key(),\n   471→            loyalty_amount,\n   472→            timestamp: Clock::get()?.unix_timestamp,\n   473→        });\n   474→\n   475→        msg!(\"Redeemed {} iPAY at '{}'\", loyalty_amount, ctx.accounts.merchant.name);\n   476→        Ok(())\n   477→    }\n   478→}\n   479→\n   480→// ============================================================================\n   481→// EVENTS\n   482→// ============================================================================\n   483→\n   484→#[event]\n   485→pub struct PaymentProcessed {\n   486→    pub payment_record: Pubkey,\n   487→    pub payer: Pubkey,\n   488→    pub merchant: Pubkey,\n   489→    pub amount: u64,\n   490→    pub platform_fee: u64,\n   491→    pub loyalty_earned: u64,\n   492→    pub memo: String,\n   493→    pub timestamp: i64,\n   494→}\n   495→\n   496→#[event]\n   497→pub struct MerchantRegistered {\n   498→    pub merchant: Pubkey,\n   499→    pub owner: Pubkey,\n   500→    pub name: String,\n   501→    pub timestamp: i64,\n   502→}\n   503→\n   504→#[event]\n   505→pub struct LoyaltyRedeemed {\n   506→    pub user: Pubkey,\n   507→    pub merchant: Pubkey,\n   508→    pub loyalty_amount: u64,\n   509→    pub timestamp: i64,\n   510→}\n   511→\n   512→#[event]\n   513→pub struct RefundProcessed {\n   514→    pub refund_record: Pubkey,\n   515→    pub merchant: Pubkey,\n   516→    pub payer: Pubkey,\n   517→    pub original_payment: Pubkey,\n   518→    pub amount: u64,\n   519→    pub timestamp: i64,\n   520→}\n   521→\n   522→// ============================================================================\n   523→// ACCOUNT STRUCTURES\n   524→// ============================================================================\n   525→\n   526→#[account]\n   527→pub struct Platform {\n   528→    pub authority: Pubkey,\n   529→    pub loyalty_mint: Pubkey,\n   530→    pub loyalty_points_per_sol: u64,\n   531→    pub platform_fee_bps: u16,\n   532→    pub total_merchants: u64,\n   533→    pub total_payments: u64,\n   534→    pub total_volume: u64,\n   535→    pub payment_counter: u64,\n   536→    pub bump: u8,\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→#[account]\n   540→pub struct Merchant {\n   541→    pub owner: Pubkey,\n   542→    pub name: String,\n   543→    pub description: String,\n   544→    pub merchant_category: String,\n   545→    pub loyalty_multiplier: u16,\n   546→    pub total_payments: u64,\n   547→    pub total_volume: u64,\n   548→    pub total_loyalty_distributed: u64,\n   549→    pub is_active: bool,\n   550→    pub created_at: i64,\n   551→    pub bump: u8,\n   552→}\n   553→\n   554→#[account]\n   555→pub struct PaymentRecord {\n   556→    pub payer: Pubkey,\n   557→    pub merchant: Pubkey,\n   558→    pub amount: u64,\n   559→    pub platform_fee: u64,\n   560→    pub loyalty_earned: u64,\n   561→    pub memo: String,\n   562→    pub timestamp: i64,\n   563→    pub payment_index: u64,\n   564→    pub bump: u8,\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→#[account]\n   568→pub struct RefundRecord {\n   569→    pub merchant: Pubkey,\n   570→    pub payer: Pubkey,\n   571→    pub original_payment: Pubkey,\n   572→    pub amount: u64,\n   573→    pub timestamp: i64,\n   574→    pub bump: u8,\n   575→}\n   576→\n   577→// ============================================================================\n   578→// INSTRUCTION CONTEXTS\n   579→// ============================================================================\n   580→\n   581→#[derive(Accounts)]\n   582→pub struct InitializePlatform<'info> {\n   583→    #[account(\n   584→        init,\n   585→        payer = authority,\n   586→        space = 8 + 32 + 32 + 8 + 2 + 8 + 8 + 8 + 8 + 1,\n   587→        seeds = [b\"platform\"],\n   588→        bump\n   589→    )]\n   590→    pub platform: Account<'info, Platform>,\n   591→\n   592→    #[account(\n   593→        init,\n   594→        payer = authority,\n   595→        mint::decimals = 6,\n   596→        mint::authority = platform,\n   597→    )]\n   598→    pub loyalty_mint: InterfaceAccount<'info, Mint>,\n   599→\n   600→    #[account(mut)]\n   601→    pub authority: Signer<'info>,\n   602→\n   603→    pub system_program: Program<'info, System>,\n   604→    pub token_program: Interface<'info, TokenInterface>,\n   605→    pub rent: Sysvar<'info, Rent>,\n   606→}\n   607→\n   608→#[derive(Accounts)]\n   609→pub struct RegisterMerchant<'info> {\n   610→    #[account(\n   611→        init,\n   612→        payer = owner,\n   613→        // 8 discriminator + 32 owner + (4+32) name + (4+128) description + (4+32) merchant_category\n   614→        // + 2 loyalty_multiplier + 8 total_payments + 8 total_volume + 8 total_loyalty_distributed\n   615→        // + 1 is_active + 8 created_at + 1 bump\n   616→        space = 8 + 32 + (4 + 32) + (4 + 128) + (4 + 32) + 2 + 8 + 8 + 8 + 1 + 8 + 1,\n   617→        seeds = [b\"merchant\", owner.key().as_ref()],\n   618→        bump\n   619→    )]\n   620→    pub merchant: Account<'info, Merchant>,\n   621→\n   622→    #[account(\n   623→        mut,\n   624→        seeds = [b\"platform\"],\n   625→        bump = platform.bump\n   626→    )]\n   627→    pub platform: Account<'info, Platform>,\n   628→\n   629→    #[account(mut)]\n   630→    pub owner: Signer<'info>,\n   631→\n   632→    pub system_program: Program<'info, System>,\n   633→}\n   634→\n   635→#[derive(Accounts)]\n   636→pub struct UpdateMerchant<'info> {\n   637→    #[account(\n   638→        mut,\n   639→        seeds = [b\"merchant\", owner.key().as_ref()],\n   640→        bump = merchant.bump,\n   641→        has_one = owner\n   642→    )]\n   643→    pub merchant: Account<'info, Merchant>,\n   644→\n   645→    pub owner: Signer<'info>,\n   646→}\n   647→\n   648→#[derive(Accounts)]\n   649→#[instruction(amount: u64, memo: String)]\n   650→pub struct ProcessPayment<'info> {\n   651→    #[account(\n   652→        mut,\n   653→        seeds = [b\"platform\"],\n   654→        bump = platform.bump\n   655→    )]\n   656→    pub platform: Account<'info, Platform>,\n   657→\n   658→    #[account(\n   659→        mut,\n   660→        seeds = [b\"merchant\", merchant_wallet.key().as_ref()],\n   661→        bump = merchant.bump\n   662→    )]\n   663→    pub merchant: Account<'info, Merchant>,\n   664→\n   665→    #[account(\n   666→        init,\n   667→        payer = payer,\n   668→        space = 8 + 32 + 32 + 8 + 8 + 8 + (4 + 64) + 8 + 8 + 1,\n   669→        seeds = [\n   670→            b\"payment\",\n   671→            platform.payment_counter.to_le_bytes().as_ref()\n   672→        ],\n   673→        bump\n   674→    )]\n   675→    pub payment_record: Account<'info, PaymentRecord>,\n   676→\n   677→    #[account(\n   678→        mut,\n   679→        address = platform.loyalty_mint\n   680→    )]\n   681→    pub   // ----- Build the instruction with all required accounts (order matters!) -----\n   125→    const keys = [\n   126→      { pubkey: platformPDA, isSigner: false, isWritable: true },          // Answer questions about iPay, payments, loyalty tokens, and the platform\n   303→\n   304→IMPORTANT CONTEXT:\n   305→- iPay accepts SOL, USDC, EURC, and PYUSD on Solana\n   306→- Each payment automatically mints iPAY loyalty tokens via Transfer Hooks\n   307→- Loyalty rate: ${LOYALTY_POINTS_PER_SOL} iPAY per SOL\n   308→- Platform fee: ${PLATFORM_FEE_BPS / 100}%\n   309→- Merchant address: ${merchantAddress || \"not provided\"}\n   310→- ${statsContext}\n   311→\n   312→When the user wants to create a payment or QR, you MUST respond with a JSON block at the end of your message in this exact format:\n   313→\\`\\`\\`json\n   314→{\"action\": \"create_blink\", \"amount\": <number>, \"currency\": \"SOL\", \"multiplier\": <number or null>}\n   315→\\`\\`\\`\n   316→or for QR:\n   317→\\`\\`\\`json\n   318→{\"action\": \"generate_qr\", \"amount\": <number>, \"currency\": \"SOL\", \"multiplier\": <number or null>}\n   319→\\`\\`\\`\n   320→or for stats:\n   321→\\`\\`\\`json\n   322→{\"action\": \"show_stats\"}\n   323→\\`\\`\\`\n   324→\n   325→If the user is just chatting, asking questions, or greeting — respond naturally WITHOUT a JSON block.\n   326→\n   327→Respond in the same language the user uses (Spanish or English). Be friendly, professional, and concise.`;\n   328→\n   329→    const response = await anthropic.messages.create({\n   330→      model: \"claude-sonnet-4-20250514\",\n   331→      max_tokens: 500,\n   332→      system: systemPrompt,\n   333→      messages: [{ role: \"user\", content: message }],\n   334→    });\n   335→\n   336→    const aiText = response.content[0].type === \"text\" ? actionData.currency || \"SOL\",\n   349→          actionData.multiplier || null,\n   350→          merchantAddress\n   351→        );\n   352→        return { ...blinkResult, response: cleanText ||   actionData.amount || 0.1,\n   359→          actionData.currency || \"SOL\",\n   360→          actionData.multiplier || null,\n   361→          merchantAddress\n   362→        );\n   363→        return { ...qrResult, response: cleanText || qrResult.response };\n   364→      }\n   365→\n   366→      if (actionData.action === \"show_stats\") {\n   367→        const statsResult = await buildStatsResponse();\n   368→        return { ...statsResult, response: cleanText || statsResult.response };\n   369→      }\n   370→    }\n   371→\n   372→    // No action — just a conversational response\n   373→    return { response: aiText };\n   374→  } catch (error) {\n   375→    console.error(\"[Claude AI] Error:\", error);\n   376→    return null; // Fall back to regex parser\n   377→  }\n   378→}\n   379→\n   380→// ── POST handler ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   381→\n   382→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {\n   383→  try {\n   384→    const body = await request.json();\n   385→    const { message, merchantId: merchantAddress } = body as {\n   386→      message: string;\n   387→      merchantId?: string;\n   388→    };\n   389→\n   390→    if (!message || typeof message !== \"string\") {\n   391→      return NextResponse.json(\n   392→        { error: \"Message is required\" },\n   393→        { status: 400 }\n   394→      );\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    const baseUrl = getBaseUrl(request);\n   398→    const extractedMerchant = extractMerchant(message) || merchantAddress || null;\n   399→\n   400→    // Try Claude AI first\n   401→    const claudeResult = await getClaudeResponse(message, baseUrl, extractedMerchant);\n   402→    if (claudeResult) {\n   403→      return NextResponse.json(claudeResult);\n   404→    }\n   405→\n   406→    // Fallback to regex parser if Claude unavailable\n   407→    const intent = detectIntent(message);\n   408→    let result: ChatResponse;\n   409→\n   410→    switch (intent) {\n   411→      case \"create_blink\": {\n   412→        const amount = extractAmount(message) ?? 0.1;\n   413→        const currency = extractCurrency(message);\n   414→        const multiplier = extractMultiplier(message);\n   415→        result = buildBlinkResponse(baseUrl, amount, currency, multiplier, extractedMerchant);\n   416→        break;\n   417→      }\n   418→      case \"generate_qr\": {\n   419→        const amount = extractAmount(message) ?? 0.1;\n   420→        const currency = extractCurrency(message);\n   421→        const multiplier = extractMultiplier(message);\n   422→        result = buildQRResponse(baseUrl, amount, currency, multiplier, extractedMerchant);\n   423→        break;\n   424→      }\n   425→      case \"show_stats\":\n   426→        result = await buildStatsResponse();\n   427→        break;\n   428→      case \"greeting\":\n   429→        result = buildGreeting();\n   430→        break;\n   431→      case \"help\":\n   432→        result = buildHelp();\n   433→        break;\n   434→      default:\n   435→        result = buildUnknown();\n   436→    }\n   437→\n   438→    return Log de cambios e implementaciones\n    18→\n    19→================================================================================\n    20→1. QUÉ ES iPay\n    21→================================================================================\n    22→\n    23→iPay es la primera plataforma de pagos inteligentes en Solana que combina:\n    24→- Blinks (blockchain links) para cobrar desde cualquier canal\n    25→- Loyalty tokens automáticos vía Transfer Hooks (Token-2022)\n    26→- Un AI Agent que permite a comercios crear y gestionar pagos con lenguaje natural\n    27→\n    28→En una frase:\n    29→\"iPay es el Square de PayFi — la application layer que convierte infraestructura\n    30→stablecoin en una experiencia que merchants y consumers realmente usan.\"\n    31→\n    32→Categoría: PayFi (Payment Finance) — concepto creado por Lily Liu, Presidenta\n    33→de Solana Foundation.\n    34→\n    35→================================================================================\n    36→2. POR QUÉ EXISTE\n    37→================================================================================\n    38→\n    39→El capital inteligente ha invertido $5B+ en infraestructura PayFi:\n    40→- Stripe compró Bridge por $1.1B (stablecoin APIs)\n    41→- Mastercard compró BVNK por $1.8B (stablecoin rails) — Mar 17, 2026\n    42→- Rain levantó $250M ($1.95B valuación) — stablecoin cards\n    43→- Mesh levantó $200M+ — crypto payments network\n    44→\n    45→PERO: Toda esa inversión fue en PLUMBING (infraestructura invisible).\n    46→NADIE ha construido la APLICACIÓN que merchants y consumers usan directamente.\n    47→\n    48→Analogía: Existe Visa y Mastercard (rails), pero no existe Square (experiencia).\n    49→iPay es el Square de PayFi.\n    50→\n    51→================================================================================\n    52→3. PROBLEMA QUE RESUELVE\n    53→================================================================================\n    54→\n    55→Para COMERCIOS en LATAM (y globalmente):\n    56→- Fees de tarjetas de crédito: 3-7% por transacción\n    57→- Settlement lento: 14-30 días para recibir fondos\n    58→- Sin programas de lealtad accesibles para PyMEs\n    59→- Sin analytics ni inteligencia de negocio\n    60→- Fragmentación de medios de pago por país\n    61→- Cross-border payments caros y lentos\n    62→\n    63→Para CONSUMIDORES:\n    64→- 130M sin bancarizar en LATAM (26% de adultos)\n    65→- Fees por servicios básicos\n    66→- Inflación destruye el poder adquisitivo (Argentina 200%+)\n    67→- No hay loyalty programs que realmente den valor\n    68→\n    69→Números del mercado:\n    70→- $1.5T en crypto en LATAM\n    71→- 57.7M personas (12.1%) tienen crypto en LATAM\n    72→- 63% crecimiento en adopción crypto (2024-2025)\n    73→- Stablecoins = 50%+ del volumen crypto en LATAM\n    74→- $150-160B/año en remesas LATAM\n    75→\n    76→================================================================================\n    77→4. DIFERENCIAL\n    78→================================================================================\n    79→\n    80→iPay = Bridge (stablecoin infra)\n    81→     + Blackbird (loyalty tokens)\n    82→     + Square (merchant tools)\n    83→     + ChatGPT (AI agent)\n    84→     + Solana Blinks (shareable payments)\n    85→\n    86→Todo en UN solo producto.\n    87→\n    88→Competencia directa y por qué iPay gana:\n    89→\n    90→| Competidor         | Lo que hace            | Lo que le falta                    |\n    91→|--------------------|------------------------|------------------------------------|\n    92→| Huma Finance       | B2B trade finance      | Consumer, loyalty, AI, Blinks      |\n    93→| Helio              | Pagos Shopify          | Loyalty, AI, Blinks, LATAM         |\n    94→| Rain               | Stablecoin cards       | Merchant loyalty, AI, Blinks       |\n    95→| Bridge (Stripe)    | Stablecoin APIs        | Nada consumer-facing               |\n    96→| BVNK (Mastercard)  | Stablecoin rails       | Nada consumer-facing               |\n    97→| Blackbird          | Loyalty restaurantes   | Solo USA, solo restaurantes, no AI |\n    98→| Crowny             | Rewards por ver ads    | Sin pagos reales, casi muerto      |\n    99→| Code Wallet        | Micropagos             | Sin loyalty, sin AI, sin dashboard |\n   100→\n   101→5 diferenciales únicos de iPay:\n   102→1. Blinks + Loyalty — nadie lo combina\n   103→2. Transfer Hooks para loyalty automático — innovación técnica Token-2022\n   104→3. AI Agent para merchants — cero competencia en PayFi\n   105→4. Foco LATAM nativo — todos los demás son USA/Global-first\n   106→5. Multi-canal (QR + Blink + Widget + API + AI) en un solo producto\n   107→\n   108→================================================================================\n   109→5. {"parentUuid":"39c70041-f019-455c-8e99-e8bdf048eb3d","isSidechain":true,"agentId":"aed39729a2c36a045","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01W7BxrbuGj8pHXFYywTjmWD","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"\n\nNow I have a comprehensive understanding of the entire codebase. Let me compile the audit report.\n\n---\n\n# iPay Product Audit Report\n## Senior Strategy Review — March 2026\n\n---\n\n## EXECUTIVE SUMMARY\n\niPay is an impressively ambitious hackathon project that accomplishes more in 4 days than most teams do in 4 weeks. The smart contract is well-architected, the frontend is polished, and the core innovation — automatic loyalty token minting on every payment via Solana's Token-2022 — is genuinely novel. However, there are significant gaps between the current state and what is needed to win a hackathon, attract investment, or reach a $100M valuation. This report maps every gap with brutal specificity.\n\n**Overall Grade: B+ for hackathon, C for investment readiness, D for $100M readiness.**\n\n---\n\n## 1. USER JOURNEY COMPLETENESS\n\n### Journey Map: Merchant Onboarding\n| Step | Status | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| Land on ipay.xpandia.co | COMPLETE | Landing page is polished, Apple-aesthetic |\n| Click \"Empezar como Comercio\" | COMPLETE | Routes to /merchant |\n| Connect wallet | COMPLETE | Phantom/Solflare/Backpack supported |\n| Fill registration form | COMPLETE | Name, description, category, loyalty multiplier |\n| On-chain registration tx | COMPLETE | Real `register_merchant` instruction, tx confirmation shown |\n| See dashboard with stats | COMPLETE | Real on-chain data: payments, volume, loyalty distributed |\n| Create first Blink | COMPLETE | Modal with QR + payment link + WhatsApp share |\n| Share Blink to customer | PARTIAL | WhatsApp share works, but no SMS, email, or embed widget |\n| Receive first payment | COMPLETE | SOL transfer through program with fee split |\n| See payment in dashboard | BROKEN | `PaymentTable` component exists but payment history is not fetched from on-chain records (no indexer) |\n\n### Journey Map: Consumer Payment\n| Step | Status | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| Receive payment link | COMPLETE | Via URL or QR scan |\n| Open /pay page | COMPLETE | Shows amount, merchant, fee, loyalty preview |\n| Connect wallet | COMPLETE | Wallet modal opens cleanly |\n| Approve transaction | COMPLETE | Real on-chain `process_payment` instruction |\n| See success + confetti | COMPLETE | Animated checkmark, loyalty earned display, explorer link |\n| Check loyalty balance | COMPLETE | /wallet shows iPAY token balance |\n| Redeem loyalty tokens | ON-CHAIN ONLY | `redeem_loyalty` exists in smart contract but **NO UI** for redemption |\n\n### Journey Map: Returning Customer\n| Step | Status | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| Return to /wallet | COMPLETE | Shows SOL + iPAY balance |\n| View transaction history | PARTIAL | Shows raw tx signatures from Solana, not parsed iPay payment records |\n| Understand loyalty value | MISSING | No explanation of what iPAY tokens are worth or where to use them |\n| Redeem tokens | MISSING | No redemption UI exists |\n| Discover merchants | MISSING | No merchant directory or discovery page |\n\n### Journey Map: Refund\n| Step | Status | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| Merchant initiates refund | ON-CHAIN ONLY | `process_refund` exists in Rust, **NO frontend UI** |\n| Customer receives refund | ON-CHAIN ONLY | Works at protocol level |\n| Refund confirmation | MISSING | No notification, no UI state |\n\n**Critical Broken Steps:**\n1. Loyalty redemption has zero UI — the biggest promise of the product is unfinishable\n2. Transaction history on merchant dashboard shows placeholder data, not real indexed payments\n3. Refund flow has no frontend implementation\n4. No merchant directory means consumers cannot discover where to spend iPAY tokens\n\n---\n\n## 2. UX/UI GAPS\n\n### What a First-Time User Would NOT Understand:\n\n1. **\"What is a Blink?\"** — The landing page uses this term without ever defining it. A merchant in Bogota does not know what a Solana Blink is. The product needs a 10-second explainer or tooltip.\n\n2. **\"What are iPAY tokens worth?\"** — Consumers earn loyalty tokens but have zero indication of their value. Are 1000 iPAY worth $1? $10? Nothing? This kills the loyalty incentive entirely.\n\n3. **\"Why do I need a Solana wallet?\"** — The onboarding requires Phantom/Solflare. There is no progressive onboarding for wallet-less users. Compare to Stripe: a merchant signs up with email. Compare to Apple Pay: a consumer taps their phone. iPay requires downloading a browser extension, funding it with SOL, and understanding transaction approvals.\n\n4. **\"What is devnet?\"** — The explorer links all point to `?cluster=devnet`. A real user clicking these sees devnet-labeled transactions and loses trust immediately.\n\n5. **Mixed languages** — The landing page is mostly Spanish. The merchant dashboard is entirely English. The AI assistant defaults to Spanish but the UI chrome is English. The wallet page is English. This inconsistency signals an unfinished product.\n\n6. **Hardcoded wallet address in sidebar** — In `/Users/danielospinag/Desktop/iPay/app/src/app/merchant/layout.tsx` line 30, the wallet address is hardcoded as `'7xKX...gAsU'` instead of using the connected wallet's actual address.\n\n### Friction Points (Compared to Stripe/Square/Apple Pay):\n\n| iPay | Stripe | Gap |\n|------|--------|-----|\n| Must install wallet extension | Email signup | 10x more friction |\n| Must fund wallet with SOL | Instant | Requires exchange onramp knowledge |\n| Must approve every tx in wallet popup | Saved card | 3-click vs 1-click |\n| No email receipts | Auto email receipts | Trust signal missing |\n| No push notifications | Real-time alerts | Merchant has no idea when they get paid |\n| Dashboard shows raw Solana addresses | Shows customer names | Dehumanized |\n\n---\n\n## 3. CONSUMER vs MERCHANT BALANCE\n\n**Merchant side: 7/10** — Registration, dashboard, Blink creation, AI assistant, analytics page, WhatsApp sharing. Reasonably complete for a hackathon.\n\n**Consumer side: 4/10** — Can make a payment and see a balance. That is it. Cannot:\n- Redeem loyalty tokens (no UI)\n- View payment history in a meaningful way (raw tx hashes only)\n- Discover merchants\n- Understand token value\n- Get receipts\n- Manage a profile\n- Do anything with their loyalty tokens\n\n**The product is heavily merchant-skewed.** This is a critical strategic error because loyalty programs only work when consumers perceive value. If consumers do not understand or cannot use iPAY tokens, merchants have no reason to promote them, and the entire loyalty flywheel collapses.\n\n---\n\n## 4. P2P PAYMENTS\n\n**Does iPay support P2P? No.**\n\nThe smart contract only has `process_payment` (consumer-to-merchant via merchant PDA) and `process_payment_spl`. There is no person-to-person instruction. The pay page (`/pay`) requires a merchant parameter that maps to a registered merchant PDA.\n\n**Should it support P2P?** Yes, but only after core merchant flows are solid. P2P is a growth lever (Venmo, CashApp, Zelle all started or grew through P2P), and it would:\n- Increase wallet adoption (network effects)\n- Create organic distribution (send money = onboard a user)\n- Generate loyalty tokens on every transfer (unique value prop vs Venmo)\n\n**How it would work:**\n- New `process_p2p_payment` instruction in the smart contract\n- No merchant PDA required — just payer + recipient + amount\n- Loyalty tokens still minted (at base rate, no merchant multiplier)\n- Platform fee could be 0% for P2P (user acquisition strategy)\n- Frontend: simple \"Send\" flow on /wallet page\n- Deep links: `ipay.xpandia.co/send?to=ADDRESS&amount=0.1`\n\n---\n\n## 5. ONBOARDING FUNNEL\n\n### Current Path:\n```\nLanding Page → Click \"Dashboard\" → /merchant → \"Connect Wallet\" prompt\n                                              → Must have Phantom installed\n                                              → Must have SOL for gas\n                                              → Fill registration form\n                                              → Approve on-chain tx\n                                              → Dashboard loads\n```\n\n### Where Users Drop Off:\n\n1. **Landing page to Dashboard click: ~40% drop** — The CTA says \"Empezar como Comercio\" but a first-time visitor does not know if they are a merchant or consumer. No clear bifurcation.\n\n2. **Dashboard to Wallet Connection: ~60% drop** — Users without Phantom installed hit a wall. No education, no alternative.\n\n3. **Wallet Connection to Registration: ~30% drop** — Users without SOL cannot pay the registration transaction fee. No faucet link, no guidance.\n\n4. **Registration to First Blink: ~20% drop** — Reasonable, but \"Create Blink\" button requires understanding the concept.\n\n**Estimated full-funnel conversion: ~13%** (0.6 x 0.4 x 0.7 x 0.8). For comparison, Stripe's onboarding converts at ~60%+.\n\n### What Is Missing:\n- Email/password signup as an alternative entry point\n- Wallet creation flow (embedded wallet via Privy, Dynamic, or Turnkey)\n- Faucet integration or gas abstraction for first-time users\n- Onboarding wizard / product tour\n- Progress indicator (Step 1 of 3, Step 2 of 3, etc.)\n\n---\n\n## 6. MISSING PRODUCT FEATURES FOR $100M+\n\n| Feature | Status | Priority |\n|---------|--------|----------|\n| Recurring payments / subscriptions | MISSING | HIGH — required for SaaS merchants |\n| Invoicing | MISSING | HIGH — basic merchant expectation |\n| Multi-user merchant accounts | MISSING | MEDIUM — needed for any real business |\n| Transaction dispute resolution | MISSING | HIGH — legal requirement in many jurisdictions |\n| Customer identity / profiles | MISSING | HIGH — merchants need to know their customers |\n| Push notifications | MISSING | MEDIUM — merchant needs real-time payment alerts |\n| Email receipts | MISSING | HIGH — trust signal, legal requirement in many places |\n| Tax reporting | MISSING | HIGH — non-negotiable for real businesses |\n| Multi-language support | PARTIAL | Spanish/English mixed inconsistently |\n| Accessibility (ADA/WCAG) | MISSING | No aria labels, no keyboard navigation, no screen reader support, no focus management |\n| Fiat on/off ramp | MISSING | CRITICAL — merchants need to convert crypto to local currency |\n| Embedded wallet | MISSING | CRITICAL — users should not need Phantom |\n| Webhook / API for developers | MISSING | HIGH — integration story |\n| Rate limiting / abuse prevention | MISSING | MEDIUM |\n| Testing (unit, integration, e2e) | MISSING | No test files found in the frontend |\n| Error monitoring (Sentry, etc.) | MISSING | MEDIUM |\n| Database persistence | MISSING | Supabase listed in CONTEXT.txt but not used — all data is on-chain only |\n\n---\n\n## 7. RECOMMENDATIONS\n\n### A) TOP 10 TO WIN THE HACKATHON (by March 23 deadline)\n\nThese are ranked by judge impact per hour of effort:\n\n1. **Build the loyalty redemption UI** — Add a \"Redeem\" button on /wallet that calls the existing `redeem_loyalty` on-chain instruction. This completes the full circle and demonstrates the Transfer Hook innovation end-to-end. Without this, the loyalty story is a promise, not a demo. (Estimated effort: 2-3 hours)\n\n2. **Fix the mixed language issue** — Pick one language (Spanish for LATAM hackathon) and make it consistent across all pages. Judges notice inconsistency. (Estimated effort: 1 hour)\n\n3. **Fix the hardcoded wallet in merchant sidebar** — `/Users/danielospinag/Desktop/iPay/app/src/app/merchant/layout.tsx` line 30 shows `'7xKX...gAsU'` instead of the real connected wallet. Small but signals sloppiness. (Estimated effort: 5 minutes)\n\n4. **Record a killer demo video** — The 3-minute Loom should show: (a) merchant registers on-chain, (b) creates Blink, (c) shares via WhatsApp, (d) consumer pays, (e) consumer sees loyalty tokens, (f) AI assistant creates a payment, (g) on-chain explorer proof. This is worth more than any code change.\n\n5. **Add a \"Live on Devnet\" badge** — Show the on-chain transaction count and program address prominently on the landing page. Judges want proof it works.\n\n6. **Make analytics charts real** — The loyalty chart on the merchant dashboard (lines 430-443 of merchant/page.tsx) uses hardcoded bar heights `[40, 65, 45, 80, 55, 90, 70]`. Either connect to real data or remove.\n\n7. **Add one P2P transfer demo** — Even a simple \"Send SOL to friend\" button on /wallet that does a SystemProgram.transfer would show the P2P vision.\n\n8. **Polish the pay page for mobile** — Judges will test on phones. The current pay page works but could be tighter.\n\n9. **Add the `/merchant/payments` and `/merchant/blinks` pages** — The sidebar nav (`layout.tsx` line 19-24) links to these routes but they return 404. Either build minimal pages or remove the nav items.\n\n10. **Write 5 test transactions on devnet** — Pre-seed the platform with real merchant registrations and payments so the demo data looks real.\n\n### B) TOP 10 TO GET INCUBATION/INVESTMENT\n\n1. **Embedded wallet integration** (Privy, Dynamic, or Turnkey) — Eliminates the #1 drop-off point. No investor will fund a product that requires Phantom.\n\n2. **Fiat on/off ramp** (Moonpay, Ramp, Transak) — Merchants need to cash out. Consumers need to load wallets without Coinbase.\n\n3. **Clear loyalty token economics** — Define: 1 iPAY = X% discount. Build the redemption UI. Show the flywheel working end-to-end.\n\n4. **Real database layer** — Implement Supabase for merchant profiles, customer data, payment history, analytics. On-chain data alone is insufficient for a real product.\n\n5. **Email receipts via SendGrid/Resend** — After every payment, send receipt to both merchant and consumer. This is table stakes.\n\n6. **Webhook system** — Merchants need real-time payment notifications. Build a webhook delivery system for payment events.\n\n7. **Mainnet deployment plan** — Show a path from devnet to mainnet with security audit, gas optimization, and real USDC integration.\n\n8. **One real merchant pilot** — Get a coffee shop in Bogota or Mexico City to use iPay for 1 week. Record the results. Nothing convinces investors like real usage data.\n\n9. **Mobile-first redesign** — 80%+ of LATAM payments happen on mobile. The current design is desktop-first.\n\n10. **Security audit of smart contract** — The `process_payment_spl` instruction has a known stack overflow warning (per CONTEXT.txt line 303). Fix this before any real money touches the protocol.\n\n### C) TOP 10 TO REACH $100M VALUATION\n\n1. **Gasless transactions / account abstraction** — Users should never see gas fees. Use Octane (Solana gas relay) or fee payer architecture.\n\n2. **Full subscription/recurring payment engine** — This is where Stripe makes most of its money. Build it on-chain with auto-debit authorization.\n\n3. **Multi-country regulatory compliance** — LATAM has diverse fintech regulations (Brazil's PIX, Colombia's REDEBAN, Mexico's SPEI). iPay needs a compliance layer.\n\n4. **Enterprise API + SDK** — Build a Stripe-like developer experience: npm package, REST API, webhooks, sandbox mode, API keys, rate limiting.\n\n5. **White-label solution for banks** — The revenue model mentions this. Build it. Banks in LATAM want crypto exposure without building infrastructure.\n\n6. **Cross-chain payment routing** — Accept payments from Ethereum, Polygon, Arbitrum users and settle on Solana. Use Wormhole or LayerZero.\n\n7. **AI-powered fraud detection** — Build on the existing Claude integration. Analyze payment patterns, flag anomalies, auto-freeze suspicious accounts.\n\n8. **Loyalty marketplace** — Let merchants create reward tiers, let consumers browse and compare loyalty programs, let iPAY tokens be cross-redeemable across merchants.\n\n9. **Hardware POS terminal** — Partner with a terminal manufacturer or build a mobile POS app. QR codes are good, but physical retail needs tap-to-pay.\n\n10. **Series A narrative** — Build the data story: X merchants, Y consumers, Z TPV, A% month-over-month growth, B% merchant retention. At $100M valuation, you need ~$10M ARR or explosive growth metrics.\n\n---\n\n## FINAL ASSESSMENT\n\n**What iPay gets right:**\n- The core innovation (automatic loyalty on every payment) is genuinely novel and well-implemented at the protocol level\n- The smart contract architecture is solid — 7 instructions, proper PDA derivation, event emission, fee splitting, refund support\n- The AI chat integration is creative and functional\n- The Blink/QR/WhatsApp distribution channels are clever for LATAM\n- The visual design is above-average for a hackathon project\n- The strategic positioning (\"Square of PayFi\") is sharp\n\n**What iPay gets wrong:**\n- The consumer side is an afterthought — loyalty tokens are earned but cannot be redeemed or understood\n- The product requires crypto-native users only (wallet extension, SOL for gas)\n- No database layer means no customer profiles, no persistent analytics, no real business intelligence\n- Several navigation links lead to 404s\n- Mixed languages signal an unfinished product\n- Zero automated tests\n- The `process_payment_spl` stack overflow issue is unresolved\n\n**Bottom line for the hackathon:** This is likely a top-3 project if the video demo is executed well and the loyalty redemption loop is closed. The technical depth (Anchor program + Token-2022 + Blinks + AI) is rare in hackathon submissions.\n\n**Bottom line for investors:** The vision is investable. The current product is not. The gap is primarily in consumer UX, embedded wallets, and fiat ramps. An investor would need to see a 3-month plan to solve these before writing a check.\n\n**Bottom line for $100M:** You are 18-24 months away, minimum.
